 00 - End kya aap apane mobile, televijan yaa tablet kaa adhik istemaal karte hai? agar karte hai to ise kam kar dijie, kyonki electronic screen aapaki neend uda sakate hai
 a recent research has revealed that the excessive use of light emitted from electronic screens can affect the sleep of adolescents
 road island sthit brown uniwarsity ke shodhakartaaon ne apane shodh main paaya ki adhik aayu ke yuvak / yuvatiyon kii apeksha 9 se 15 varsh ke bich ke kishoron or kishoriyon kii neend screen kii roshan ke prati zyada samvedansheel hoti he
 From experiments conducted in the laboratory, the researchers found that the strong light emitted by electronic overtones at night reduces the sleep hormone 'melatonin' in adolescents
 jitani tej roshni hogi utana hi in hormones par asar padegaa
 The comments manochikitsa or maanav vyavhaar kii professor or lekhika mairi karskadon ne kaha ki raat main mobile or anya upkarnon se nikali kam maatra kii roshni bhi neend ko prabhavit karne ke liye kaaphi he
 This makes it very difficult to sleep at night and to get up early for school in the morning
 bacchon or unke abhibhavakon ko sote samay apane electronic upkarnon kaa istemaal kam karnaa chahie
 The research was published in the journal 'clinical Endocrinology and Metabolism'
 ek taaja shodh main yah saamne aayaa he ki electronic screen se nikalne vaali roshni kaa adhik istemaal kishoron kii neend par bura asar daal sakati he
 Researchers at Rhode Island-based Brown University found in their research that adolescents and adolescents between 9 and 15 years of age are more sensitive to sleep screen than older men / young people
 prayogshaala main kiye gaye prayogon se shodhakartaaon ne paaya ki raat main electronic uparkarnon se nikalne vaali tej roshni kishoron main neend ke hormone 'melatonin' ko kam kar detaa he
 The stronger the light, the greater the impact on these hormones
 tippaniyan Mary Karskadon, professor and author of psychiatry and human behavior, said the low amount of light emitted from mobiles and other devices at night is also enough to affect sleep
 isse raat ko neend aane main or subah skool ke liye jaldi uthne main kaaphi mushkil hoti he

 Devdatta Patnaik's book 'myth = Mithya' seeks answers to the contradictions between life and death, nature and culture, excellence and possibility
 ve apni anokhi lekhan style, drushtaanton or chitron ke jariye hindu kahaniyon ko prastut karte hai or hindu pratikon or reeti-rivaajon kii gutthiyaan sulajhaate hai
 Through this we can know why the Kauravas reached heaven and (except Yudhishthira) all the Pandavas in hell; Why Rama, who renounced Sita, was considered an ideal king; How did black drinkers become another form of black milk-giving Gauri; And why Shiva separated the fifth head of Brahma from the torso
 doctor devdatt patnayak kii charchit kitaab myth baraabar mithyaa kaa hindi main anuwaad kiya he alok kumaar ne
 Originally published in English, the book has sold 70 thousand copies so far
 ab penguin ne ise hindi main prakashit karne kaa faisla kiya he

 ajey durga: devdatt patnayakadi-maaya-shakti kii pratik durga ajey hai
 He is also a bride and a warrior at the same time
 ve ek rup main ghar sthapit karti hai, sukh detii hai, bachche paidaa karti hai or bhojan uplabdh karaati hai
 In another form she goes to the battlefield and commits murders
 jo unki sharan main aata he uski raksha karti hai or jo chunauti detaa he uskaa sanhaar karti hai
 She also calms down the lion and makes him ride
 vah apane kesh kabhi nahin baandhti
 Mahishasura King Mahishasura of the Vadasuras succeeded in taking a boon from Brahma, after which he could not kill any tree plant, animal, man, demon or god
 shaktishaalee mahisasur ne devon ko nabh mandal se bhaga diya
 He went to his father Brahma
 brahma ne unhen vishnu or vishnu ne shiv ke paas bheja
 Shiva instructed all the Devas to draw out their powers and build power by gathering
 devon ne aag kii lapaton ke rup main apni shaktiyaan baahar nikaalin jinamein se aath haathon vaali yoddha devi durga prakat huin jinaki sawari sher thi
 Mahish fell in love with her and wanted to make her his wife
 mahish ne apane duuton ko is sandesh ke saath unke paas bheja
 Durga replied that she would be able to get married only if she defeated them in a fight
 mahish ne kai ladaake unhen laane ke liye bheje lekin ve naakaam rahe
 Goddess killed everyone one by one
 ant main mahish ne un par dhaava bol diya
 For this, he was wearing animals
 singh, hathi, bhens banakar vah hamalaa kar rahaa tha
 After a fierce battle that lasted nine nights, Durga killed her with a trident and ended her illusion
 vah isliye safal raheen ki mahish ne mahila se jivan raksha kaa vardaan nahin liya tha
 (markandeya Purana) Whether the death of Asura and Devamishasura or the death of another Asura, the peace after this did not last long
 jald hi koi nayaa asur utpann hota tha or jeet haar kaa chakra chalata rahaa
 It seems that the fight was a reaction to peace and its reverse process was also carried on
 devon or asuron kii badalati kismat main ek tarah kaa lay he
 Nobody is defeated forever
 donon barabari karte dikhte hai
 It indicates that the Asuras are also necessary for the existence of the world
 unke bina koi santulan nahin rahegaa
 God never destroys Asuras
 asur ko sirf uski jagah dikhaa di jaati he
 In the Hindu world, Asuras live in Hiranyapur, a city built in Hades under the earth
 dev akaash ke upar bane shahar amravati main rahete hai
 The place between the two worlds is the battleground
 neeche baali kii kahani he jo dayaalu tha par dharti ke upar uski upasthiti se teenon lokon kaa santulan bighad gaya
 The system was restored only when Shiva showed her his place, that is, sent him down to the earth
 asuron ke raja baalivishaal rup dhaaran kar teenon lokon par vijay pataakaa fahraane vaale vishnu trivikram kehalaae
 Bali, the king of the Asuras sent to the Hades, comes up every year at harvest time
 kerala main unke upar aane ko olym parv ke taur par manaaya jaataa he
 On the other hand, celebrate Diwali on this occasion in North India
 dilachasp rup se fasalon se jude har parv kaa sambandh asuron kii maut se he
 Dussehra is a symbol of Mahishasura slaughter at the hands of Durga and Diwali is related to the defeat of Bali at the hands of hell and Trivikram at the hands of Krishna
 asuron kii maut kaa fasalon kii kataai ke parvon se sambandh koi aise hi nahin he
 As a foster of Sanjeevani Vidya, the Asuras continue to restore the fertility of the earth
 or asur ko maarane ke baad or fasal kaatane se hi dharaa kii dein ko apane hisse main kiya ja saktaa he
 The relation of the Asuras to the Hades and harvesting of crops, the kindness of Bali and the fact that his city is made of gold indicates that the Asuras are the custodians of wealth
 sabhi dhan chaahe wo paudha ho yaa jaanavar yaa khanij sabaki utpatti dharti ke neeche se hi he
 Even Lakshmi is said to live in Hades
 dev asuron ke pataal main rakhe dhan ko jari karte hai
 The Sun God helps plants grow skyward with their heat and light
 chandra bhagwaan samudr kii tarangon par niyantran rakhte hai jisase machhlee maarane or namak nikaalane main madad milti he
 Indra, the god of the sky, sends a monsoon cloud that causes rain
 hawa ke devtaa vaayu pahaado se nadiyon ko neeche utaarne main madad karte hai
 The fire gods melt the fire stones from which the metal comes out
 asuron ko us sthiti main adhik taqatvar mana jaataa he jab surya dakshinyan hokar kark raashi se makar raashi kii ore rukh karata he
 Then the days become shorter and the nights become colder
 jab chand chota hone lagata he tab bhi asuron kii takat badhati he
 Asuras are more powerful at night
 devon ke saath asur din, maheene or saal kaa chakra puraa karte hai
 Shiva and Shaktimosam come, go
 samskruti kaa utthan or patan hota he
 Prices change
 maanak parivartaneey hai
 Earthly truths appear to be associated with conditions
 yah sthaan, samay or logon ke vichaaron ke saapekshik he
 Shiva is the God who does not believe in these worldly truths
 vah us sachai ko khojate hai jo sthaayee he, purna he or bina shart he
 Therefore, he keeps his eyes closed on behalf of the world
 vah yaadon, ichchhaaon, vichaaron or ahm ko apane chitt main sthaan dene se manaa karte hai
 The purity of the mind leads to enlightenment
 gyanoday ke saath aata he anand, shantipurna vardaan
 This boon is above all desires
 mahasoos karne or pratikriya dene kii koi lalak nahin he
 There is no need for body or even world
 koi kriya, pratikriya yaa javabdehi nahin he
 There is no karma, so there is no world
 vishwa kaa astitv nahin he
 All that exists is a soul that is in solitude created for itself
 isliye shiv vishwa ke sanhaarak bhagwaan hai
 One is a number that is soulless, Ussar
 jab sirf ek hi hota he tab na koi pyaar hota he, na chahat na sangam
 Any relationship requires at least two to form
 duusare ke bina khud kaa koi vajood nahin he
 Maya is needed to feel the truth or truth; Maya means worldly truths with conditions
 aatma ke maun ko samajhane ke liye urja kii bechaini kii jarurat he
 The Goddess is Maya who assimilates all illusions
 vah shakti hai, urja kaa vyaktiparak rup
 They are etc
 matlab utani pracheen or seemaheen jitani aatma
 She can be as wild and scary as Kali, depending on time, place, and decisions
 par duusari ore utani hi dayaalu or pyaari ho sakati hai jaisi gauri hai
 She is the world from which Shiva has kept himself away
 vah unke dil main pyaar laane kii koshish karegi, ankhen kholane par majaboor karengi or sansaarik jivan main laane kii koshish hogi
 Love will make the divine innermost contact with the divine outer world
 ye lalak or sangam sabhi chizon ke astitv ko vaidhata pradaan karegaa

 gaanv ke log kehete hai ki librari kab khulti he kisi ko pataa nahin
 On October 11, when leaders come or a big leader comes, there is a stir, after which the library is closed
 librari ke aage ek murti bani he
 Nitish Kumar also started paying pension to five thousand people who were jailed during Emergency by creating JP Army
 2011 main anna andolan ke samay jab adwani ne yahaan se kalaadhan ke kilaaf apni rath yatra shuru kii tab nitish kumaar bhi unke saath the
 Due to this chariot journey, electricity also reached the village, which now comes seven to eight hours
 lekin chaar saal ke bheetar nitish kumaar ko bijepi se alag hona padaa or jayaprabha foundation ke pramukh gajendra singh mast bijepi ke tikat par chunaav ladane chale gaye
 Memorials have been a part of our electoral politics
 jepi kii us raajnneeti kaa kya hashr hua uskaa koi eemaandaar vishleshan hoga isaki to ummid mat hi rakhiye
 There is no dearth of institutes for research on democracy, panchayat and Gandhi, but no one comes other than the leaders on October 11, but there is no electoral construction of a museum memorial there
 dhire-dhire log likhane lagenge ki is faisle ke zariye lalu or nitish ke paale se jepi kii viraasat ko hadapaa jayega lekin gaur se aap dekhenge ki jepi ke jo bhi sinddhant the un par koi nahin chal rahaa he
 No one is following the path of Gandhi and Patel, only memorials are being built in their name
 tippaniyan It is not that this country has forgotten Jayaprakash Narayan
 - jai prakaash narayan international airport patna - Loknayak Jayaprakash Hospital Ortho, Patna - jaiprakash university, chhapra, bihar - Lok Nayak Jayaprakash National Institute of Criminology and Forensic Science, Delhi - lokanayak jaiprakash aspataal, dilli - Jayaprakash Narayan Trauma Center, AIIMS - lokanayak bhawan jisamen rashtriya anusuchit ayog kaa daftar he - Loknayak Jaiprakash Park, Bahadur Shah Zafar Marg, Delhi - lokanayak jaiprakash aspataal, kusht nivaaran trust, mumbai - Jayaprakash Narayan College of Engineering, Mahbubnagar, Andhra Pradesh - jai prakaash narayan baio diaversity park, karnataka - Jai Prakash Narayan PU College, Shimoga, Karnataka iske alaava desh ke tamaam shaharon main aapako jepi nagar mil jaayegaa
 Memorial and trust are not lacking
 ho saktaa ki bihar kii raajnneeti ke kaaran jepi kii bhi hazaron foot oonchi pratimaa kaa elaan ho jaae lekin kya kabhi ham khulkar baat kar paayenge ki us andolan main sabakuch mahaan yaa adarsh nahin tha
 What can be done if we have considered the glory of the past as political destiny
 uttar se lekar dakshin tak kai netaaon ke naam par santhaan memorial or park bane hai
 a separate memorial or institute should be formed to study what has benefited politics from this and what has benefited democracy from the studies done there
 jai prakaash narayan kaa janm sitab diyaara ke 32 tolon main se ek lalapura tolaa main hua tha lekin baadh ke baad ve uttar pradesh ke hisse vaale sitab diyaara main aa gaye or vahiin rahe
 In this part, a JP trust was formed by former Prime Minister Chandrasekhar in his name
 is trust kii imaarat kaaphi thikthak he
 jp's books, photographs, chair, bed, etc
 are kept in it
 jab tak chandrashekhar zindaa the tab tak yahaan 11 aktubar ko har saal mela jaisaa lagata rahaa jisamen kai bade netaa jamaa hote rahe
 Now this trust is occupied by his family's Ravi Shankar Singh Pappu, who is currently a councilor from Bahujan Samaj Party
 chandrashekhar ke bete niraj shekhar samaajawaadee party se rajya sabha ke saansad hai
 The village comes in Ballia district, whose MP is bjp's Bharat Singh
 gaanv ke log kehete hai ki trust par dabangon kaa kabza ho gaya he
 It no longer opens to the public, only when MLC Ravi Shankar Singh comes or wants
 isamen ek guest house bhi he
 The people of the village say that the condition of Modi government's proposal to build a memorial should not be like the JP Trust
 sitab diyaara ke upi vaale hisse main skool or aspataal to he magar vahaan shikshakon kii sankhya kam he or gaanv ke logon ne kaha ki aspataal main ek doctor he jo kabhi kabhaar hi aate hai
 Flood is the destiny of this village
 is vakt rajya sarkaar baandhon kii marammat kaa kaary kara rahi he
 Sitab Diara in UP is exactly 2 km from where JP was born
 lalapura tolaa
 Where Modi government will build a memorial
 yah hissaa bihar ke chhapra zile main aata he jiske saansad hai kendriya mantri rajeev pratap rudi
 Jayaprabha Foundation President Virendra Singh Mast has left with Prime Minister Modi
 ve ab upi ke bhadoi se saansad hai
 It is being told that there will be study and research on democracy in the Memorial
 ho saktaa he ki pradhanmantri modi udghaatan karenge
 In up's Sitab Diyara, there is a trust in jp's name, while in Bihar's Sitab Diyara in the name of his wife Jayaprabha
 ek jepi ko do hissaa nahin ho saktaa tha to upi ke hisse main pati aa gaye or bihar ke hisse main patni
 In 2010, Nitish Kumar built the Jayaprabha Foundation and built a library in this old and ruined house
 yahaan bhi jepi kii puraani kitaaben tasviren hai
 The people of the village say that no one knows when the library opens
 11 oktober ko jab netaa aate hai yaa koi bada netaa aata he to yahaan halchal hoti he, uske baad librari band ho jaati he
 a statue is built in front of the library
 nitish kumaar jepi sena banaakar apatkaal ke dauraan jail gaye paanch hazaar logon ko pension bhi dene lage
 During the Anna movement in 2011, when Advani started his Rath Yatra against black money from here, Nitish Kumar was also with him
 is rath yatra ke kaaran gaanv main bijli bhi pahunch gai jo ab saat aath ghante aati he
 But within four years Nitish Kumar had to break away from the BJP and Jayaprabha Foundation chief Gajendra Singh Mast went to contest on a BJP ticket
 memorial hamaari chunavi raajnneeti kaa ek hissaa rahaa he
 Do not expect that there will be an honest analysis of what happened to jp's politics
 loktantr, panchayat or gandhi par shodh ke liye sansthaanon kii kami nahin he lekin 11 oktober ko netaaon ke alaava sitab diyaara koi aata jaataa nahin, vahaan musium memorial bananaa chunavi nahin to or kya he

 tamilnadu ke tutikorin main sterlite copper ke plant ke khilaaf pradarshan kar rahe logon par golibari se 12 logon kii maut ho gai he
 The CEO of Vedanta group company Sterlite Copper has described the incident as unfortunate
 unka aarope he ki kuch swaarthee tatwon ne sthaneey logon ko gumraah kiya
 Significantly, people of the Vedanta group company Sterlite Copper were protesting against pollution from the plant for the last 100 days

 badi raashi ke lenden ke liye artijies (real time gros setlement) or do lakh rupee tak ke lenden ke liye enift (neshnal electronic fund transfar) pranali kaa upyog kiya jaataa he
 The bank said in a statement, "customers using the bank's YONO, Internet banking and mobile banking services have not been charged any fee on RTGS and NEFT transactions since July 1
" iske alaava in graahakon ko ek agast se iempies lenden par bhi koi shulk nahin dena hoga

" iske panjikrut graahakon kii sankhya kareeb ek karod he
 Apart from this, the number of customers of the Internet banking service of the bank is six crore and the number of customers of mobile banking 1
 41 karod ke aasapaas he
